        PlayFACTO School students win the ğğ”ğ“ğ’ğ“ğ€ğğƒğˆğğ† ğğ„ğ‘ğ…ğğ‘ğŒğ€ğğ‚ğ„ award!        </a></h2>
    </div>

    <div class="entry">
      <h1 class="c-h1">PlayFACTO School students win the ğğ”ğ“ğ’ğ“ğ€ğğƒğˆğğ† ğğ„ğ‘ğ…ğğ‘ğŒğ€ğğ‚ğ„ award!</h1>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-18067" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07020-300x200.jpg" alt="" width="701" height="467" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07020-300x200.jpg 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07020-768x512.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 701px) 100vw, 701px"></p>
<p>As the curtains draw over DJI RoboMaster International Game (RMIG) 2024 Hong Kong, we would like to congratulate our amazing Singapore PlayFACTO School students for bringing home the ğğ”ğ“ğ’ğ“ğ€ğğƒğˆğğ† ğğ„ğ‘ğ…ğğ‘ğŒğ€ğğ‚ğ„ award!</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-18063" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Playfacto-Article-Images-8-300x210.png" alt="" width="701" height="491" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Playfacto-Article-Images-8-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Playfacto-Article-Images-8-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Playfacto-Article-Images-8.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 701px) 100vw, 701px"></p>
<p>Our DSA team has had an incredible experience and they went all out with their dedication and teamwork against worthy opponents, from Malaysia, South Korea, Taiwan, Macau &amp; Hong Kong.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-18039" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/12-300x210.png" alt="" width="700" height="490" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/12-300x210.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/12-768x538.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/12.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 700px) 100vw, 700px"></p>
<p>We are incredibly proud of your achievements and hard work, and we look forward to welcoming you back to Singapore <img draggable="false" class="emoji" alt="ğŸ‡¸ğŸ‡¬" src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/11/svg/1f1f8-1f1ec.svg"><img draggable="false" class="emoji" alt="ğŸŒŸ" src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/11/svg/1f31f.svg"></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-18065" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07016-300x200.jpg" alt="" width="701" height="467" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07016-300x200.jpg 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/AUG07016-768x512.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 701px) 100vw, 701px"></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3>Find out more about our 53 Collaborative Learning Centres Islandwide!</h3>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-14614" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-300x300.png" alt="" width="300" height="300" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-300x300.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-150x150.png 150w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-768x768.png 768w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95-570x570.png 570w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/95.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px"></p>
<h6><span style="font-weight: 400;"><img class="wp-image-9652 size-medium alignleft" src="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1-300x94.png" alt="" width="300" height="94" srcset="https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1-300x94.png 300w, https://playfactoschool.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Website-Logo-1.png 480w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px"></span></h6>
